      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 16th century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 1600 to 1501 BC there were 225
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 78 were partial, 67 were annular (two
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 59 were total, and 21 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, in 1600 BC, 1582 BC, 1564 BC, and 1535 BC. Two months, June 1535 BC and May 1524 BC, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
